  <script>
  function initialize_wunderkind(d) {
    window.addEventListener('load', function() {
      var e = d.createElement('script');
      e.src = d.location.protocol + '//tag.wknd.ai/5453/i.js';
      e.async = true;
      d.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(e);
    });
  }

  function determine_wunderkind_eligibility() {
    if (window.location.search.includes('enable_wunderkind')) {
      initialize_wunderkind(document);
      return;
    }

    let wunderkind_segment = 0;
    try { wunderkind_segment = localStorage.getItem('genius_wunderkind_segment'); } catch (e) {}

    if (typeof(wunderkind_segment) === 'string') {
      wunderkind_segment = Number(wunderkind_segment);
    } else {
      wunderkind_segment = Math.random();
      try { localStorage.setItem('genius_wunderkind_segment', wunderkind_segment); } catch (e) {}
    }

    if ((wunderkind_segment * 100) < 100.0) {
      window['com.Genius.wunderkind_cohort'] = 'wunderkind';
      initialize_wunderkind(document);
    } else {
      window['com.Genius.wunderkind_cohort'] = 'control';
    }
  }

  determine_wunderkind_eligibility();
</script>

  <script>
    (function() {
      const anaIntegrationRolloutPercentage = 0.0

      const getCookie = (cookieKey) => {
        const cookies = document.cookie.split('; ').reduce((accum, cookie) => {
          const [key, value] = cookie.split('=')

          if (key && value) {
            accum[key] = value
          }

          return accum
        }, {})

        return cookies[cookieKey]
      }

      const setCookie = (cookieName, cookieValue, expirationInDays) => {
        const date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (expirationInDays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        const expires = "expires="+date.toUTCString();
        document.cookie = cookieName + "=" + cookieValue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
      }

      let anaIntegrationCohort = Number(
        getCookie('genius_ana_integration_rollout_cohort')
      );
      const searchParams = new URL(document.location).searchParams;

      if (!anaIntegrationCohort) {
        anaIntegrationCohort = Math.random() * 100;
        setCookie('genius_ana_integration_rollout_cohort', anaIntegrationCohort, 30);
      }

      window.useAnaAdsBundle = () => (
        searchParams.has('anaIntegration') ?
          searchParams.get('anaIntegration') !== 'false' :
          anaIntegrationCohort < anaIntegrationRolloutPercentage
      );
    })()
  </script>

        script.defer = true;

      };

      const adsBundleUrl =
        window.useAnaAdsBundle() ?
          assemblyAdsBundleUrl :
          geniusAdsBundleUrl;

      loadAdsBundle(adsBundleUrl);
    })()
  </script>

href="https://genius.com/transcribers" font-weight="light" class="StyledLink-sc-15c685a-0 lnzQV">transcribers forum</a></p></div></div></div></form></div><div class="SectionLeaderboard-sc-dbc68f4-0 dcfCGz"><div class="SectionLeaderboard-sc-dbc68f4-1 kjlIKp"><div class="DfpAd-sc-8081638d-0 dyoUOe"><div id="div-gpt-ad-desktop_song_about_leaderboard-desktop_song_about_leaderboard-1"></div><div class="DfpAd-sc-8081638d-1 iQPeOJ"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="SectionScrollSentinel-sc-8f2d21d5-0 bYYsxi"><div class="SectionScrollSentinel-sc-8f2d21d5-1 ktTqe"></div><div id="about" class="SectionScrollSentinel-sc-8f2d21d5-2 eMjUhG"></div><div class="PageGrid-desktop-sc-3faf0c7e-0 SongPageGrid-desktop-sc-b235b7c9-0 fzOXFC About-sc-9225a8f5-0 sSySO"><div class="About-sc-9225a8f5-1 eXGRwO"><h1 font-size="xxLargeHeadline" class="About-sc-9225a8f5-2 bSOkfl">About</h1><div class="SongDescription-sc-221e7474-0 WIJSj"><div class="Attribution-sc-c13c6969-0 haIGhG"><div class="Attribution-sc-c13c6969-1 cJxbKa"><span>Genius Annotation</span><button text-decoration="underline" type="button" class="TextButton-sc-5aad70cc-0 eNlUcN">22 contributors</button></div></div><div class="ExpandableContent-sc-8775ac96-0 cMZNsv"><div class="ExpandableContent-sc-8775ac96-4 jeqbuT"><div class="SongDescription-sc-221e7474-2 iWePtH"><div class="RichText-sc-3f4fe576-0 cqbmxT"><p>On the ironically braggadocious track “HUMBLE.” Kendrick Lamar challenges his competition. It was released a week after the first promotional single, <a href="https://genius.com/Kendrick-lamar-the-heart-part-4-lyrics" rel="noopener" data-api_path="/songs/3032843">“The Heart Part 4,”</a> with a music video directed by <a href="http://davemeyers.com/" rel="noopener nofollow">Dave Meyers</a> and <a href="https://genius.com/artists/The-little-homies" rel="noopener" data-api_path="/artists/822864">The Little Homies.</a> It features religious imagery mixed with urban life, such as <a href="https://genius.com/11593050" rel="noopener" data-api_path="/referents/11593050">Kendrick in priest’s robes</a> and a moving re-enactment of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leonardo_da_Vinci" rel="noopener nofollow">Leonardo Da Vinci</a>’s painting <a href="http://www.leonardodavinci.net/the-last-supper.jsp" rel="noopener nofollow"><em>The Last Supper</em></a>—juxtaposing this with the concept of humility in the chorus.</p>

<p>On a religious note, the song could also be a reference to <a href="https://www.biblegateway.com/passage/?search=james+4%3A7&amp;version=NLT" rel="noopener nofollow">James Chapter 4, verse 7</a>:</p>

<blockquote><p>So humble yourselves before God. Resist the devil, and he will flee from you.</p></blockquote>

<p><a href="https://genius.com/artists/Mike-will-made-it" rel="noopener" data-api_path="/artists/29978">Mike WiLL Made-It</a> produced the beat. It features a deep piano riff and a banging 808 bass line. This style of production is a departure from the sound of Kendrick’s previous jazz-influenced project, <a href="https://genius.com/albums/Kendrick-lamar/To-pimp-a-butterfly" rel="noopener" data-api_path="/albums/120991"><em>To Pimp a Butterfly</em></a>. It seems to reference the character Deebo’s theme song from the popular comedy movie <a href="http://bit.ly/2pA6OFH" rel="noopener nofollow"><i>Friday</i> (1995)</a>. Kendrick is also shown riding through the neighborhood on a bicycle in the music video, similar to Deebo in <i>Friday</i>.</p>

<p>The song debuted at No. 2 on the Billboard Hot 100 on April 22, 2017, making it not only the highest charting song for Kendrick, but also one of the highest debuting hip-hop singles since <a href="https://genius.com/genius.com/Eminem-love-the-way-you-lie-lyrics" rel="noopener">“Love the Way You Lie”</a> by <a href="https://genius.com/artists/Eminem" rel="noopener" data-api_path="/artists/45">Eminem</a>. The song later hit No. 1 on the chart on June 5, 2017, making it Lamar’s first solo No. 1 song and second No. 1 song overall on the charts.</p></div></div></div><div class="ExpandableContent-sc-8775ac96-3 bPwAqK"><button class="Button-sc-5e551c2c-0 gVWXZd ExpandableContent-sc-8775ac96-1 jCklyC" type="button">Expand<!-- --> <span class="InlineSvg-sc-60a40b61-0 eHSVib"><svg viewBox="0 0 6.6 16"><path d="M1.6 8.8l.6-.6 1 1 .5.7V6H0v-.8h4.5v4.6l.5-.6 1-1 .6.5L4 11.3 1.6 8.8z"></path></svg></span></button></div></div><div class="AnnotationEditActions-sc-8816f751-0 eFRGBF SongDescription-sc-221e7474-6 dcGCVc"></div><div class="AnnotationActions-sc-1c5d2834-0 iNAfbo"><div class="VotingActions-sc-7dad57be-0 pzTwZ"><svg viewBox="0 0 21.62 21.36" aria-label="upvote" aria-pressed="false" class="VotingActions-sc-7dad57be-3 hJxlPu"><path d="M16.52 21.29H6V8.5l.84-.13a3.45 3.45 0 0 0 1.82-1.09 13.16 13.16 0 0 0 .82-1.85c1.06-2.69 2-4.78 3.52-5.31a2.06 2.06 0 0 1 1.74.17c2.5 1.42 1 5 .16 6.95-.11.27-.25.6-.31.77a.78.78 0 0 0 .6.36h4.1a2.29 2.29 0 0 1 2.37 2.37c0 .82-1.59 5.4-2.92 9.09a2.39 2.39 0 0 1-2.22 1.46zm-8.52-2h8.56a.48.48 0 0 0 .31-.17c1.31-3.65 2.73-7.82 2.79-8.44 0-.22-.1-.32-.37-.32h-4.1A2.61 2.61 0 0 1 12.54 8 4.29 4.29 0 0 1 13 6.46c.45-1.06 1.64-3.89.7-4.43-.52 0-1.3 1.4-2.38 4.14a10 10 0 0 1-1.13 2.38A5.28 5.28 0 0 1 8 10.11zM0 8.4h4.86v12.96H0z"></path></svg><button color="background.positiveNumber" class="VotingActions-sc-7dad57be-1 VotingActions-sc-7dad57be-2 class="SectionScrollSentinel-sc-8f2d21d5-2 eMjUhG"></div><div class="InnerSectionDivider-sc-a74bb7a5-0 iOophZ"></div><div class="QuestionList-sc-efd94c82-0 dyvNux"><div class="QuestionList-sc-efd94c82-1 sQIah"><h2 font-size="xxLargeHeadline" class="QuestionList-sc-efd94c82-2 dQoMiC">Q&amp;A</h2><p class="QuestionList-sc-efd94c82-3 iazImu">Find answers to frequently asked questions about the song and explore its deeper meaning</p></div><div class="QuestionFormControls-sc-79859f24-1 jvLRim"><button type="button" class="Button-sc-5e551c2c-0 gVWXZd">Ask a question</button></div><div class="QuestionList-sc-efd94c82-5 eTcvdM"><div id="artist_comment:song:3039923" class="QuestionTemplate-sc-3ba252af-1 jettIo"><div class="QuestionTemplate-sc-3ba252af-4 vmFRt"><span>What did Kendrick Lamar say about &quot;HUMBLE.&quot;?</span><button class="TextButton-sc-5aad70cc-0 iFFNkr QuestionTemplate-sc-3ba252af-5 jPTlko" type="button"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M0 10h24v4h-24z"></path></svg></button></div><div class="Answer-sc-65c36c09-0 gSMdNE"><div class="Attribution-sc-c13c6969-0 haIGhG"><div class="Attribution-sc-c13c6969-1 cJxbKa"><span><div class="Answer-sc-65c36c09-3 fiyOOc">Genius Answer</div></span><button text-decoration="underline" type="button" class="TextButton-sc-5aad70cc-0 eNlUcN">2 contributors</button></div></div><div class="Answer-sc-65c36c09-1 eMbwwi"><div class="RichText-sc-3f4fe576-0 cqbmxT"><p>About a month after the song’s release, producer Mike WiLL Made-It <a href="https://www.npr.org/sections/therecord/2017/04/25/525450544/how-mike-will-made-it-and-kendrick-lamar-created-the-years-most-urgent-music-yet" rel="noopener nofollow">spoke with <i>NPR</i></a> about working with Kendrick and how the song came to be, amongst other things:</p>

<blockquote><p>With “HUMBLE.,” I knew that beat was going to capture a moment. It just felt real urgent. I made that beat [last year] when Gucci Mane was getting out of jail; I made it with him in mind. I was just thinking, damn, Gucci’s about to come home; it’s got to be something urgent that’s just going to take over the radio. And I felt like that beat was that. I ended up not doing it with Gucci and I let Kendrick hear it. I was thinking, if Dot gets on this it’ll be his first time being heard on some[thing] like this. At the same time, it kind of has an NWA/Dr. Dre feel, an Eminem kind of feel. So I thought, let me see if Dot f**** with it. And he heard the beat and he liked it. But he was about to give me “HUMBLE.” for [my album] <i>Ransom 2</i>. I love that song so I was like, ‘Man, hell yeah.’ Then he told me that his team was saying he should keep it. And I told him, ‘Bruh, you definitely should keep it, and you should use it as your single.’</p></blockquote></div></div></div><div class="QuestionAnswerActions-sc-93817617-0 hrdIsT"></div></div><div class="QuestionTemplate-sc-3ba252af-1 jettIo"><div class="QuestionTemplate-sc-3ba252af-4 vmFRt"><span>Has Kendrick ever used the phrase &quot;taste bloods&quot; before?</span><button class="TextButton-sc-5aad70cc-0 iFFNkr QuestionTemplate-sc-3ba252af-5 jPTlko" type="button"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M0 10h24v4h-24z"></path></svg></button></div><div class="Answer-sc-65c36c09-0 gSMdNE"><div class="Attribution-sc-c13c6969-0 haIGhG"><div class="Attribution-sc-c13c6969-1 cJxbKa"><span><div class="Answer-sc-65c36c09-3 fiyOOc">Genius Answer</div></span><button text-decoration="underline" type="button" class="TextButton-sc-5aad70cc-0 eNlUcN">2 contributors</button></div></div><div class="Answer-sc-65c36c09-1 eMbwwi"><div class="RichText-sc-3f4fe576-0 cqbmxT"><p>In the <a href="https://genius.com/Screen-genius-god-is-gangsta-short-film-annotated" rel="noopener" data-api_path="/songs/2399538"><em>God Is Gangsta</em></a> extended music video, there is a frame that displays the words, “My taste bloods is expensive.”</p>

<p><img src="https://images.genius.com/1aba3f57ed6446be98451fb5f081fcf2.1000x488x1.png" alt="" width="1000" height="488" data-animated="false"></p></div></div></div><div WiLL Made It collaborated before?</span><button class="TextButton-sc-5aad70cc-0 iFFNkr QuestionTemplate-sc-3ba252af-5 jPTlko" type="button"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M0 10h24v4h-24z"></path></svg></button></div><div class="Answer-sc-65c36c09-0 gSMdNE"><div class="Attribution-sc-c13c6969-0 haIGhG"><div class="Attribution-sc-c13c6969-1 cJxbKa"><span><div It was released a week after the first promotional single, “The Heart Part 4,” with a music video directed by Dave Meyers and The Little Homies. It features religious imagery mixed with urban life, such as Kendrick in priest’s robes and a moving re-enactment of Leonardo Da Vinci’s painting The Last Supper—juxtaposing this with the concept of humility in the chorus.\\n\\nOn a religious note, the song could also be a reference to James Chapter 4, verse 7:\\n\\nSo humble yourselves before God. Resist the devil, and he will flee from you.\\n\\nMike WiLL Made-It produced the beat. It features a deep piano riff and a banging 808 bass line. This style of production is a departure from the sound of Kendrick’s previous jazz-influenced project, To Pimp a Butterfly. It seems to reference the character Deebo’s theme song from the popular comedy movie Friday (1995). Kendrick is also shown riding through the neighborhood on a bicycle in the music video, similar to Deebo in Friday.\\n\\nThe song debuted at No. 2 on the Billboard Hot 100 on April 22, 2017, making it not only the highest charting song for Kendrick, but also one of the highest debuting hip-hop singles since “Love the Way You Lie” by Eminem. It was released a week after the first promotional single, [\\\"The Heart Part 4,\\\"](https://genius.com/Kendrick-lamar-the-heart-part-4-lyrics) with a music video directed by [Dave Meyers](http://davemeyers.com/) and [The Little Homies.](https://genius.com/artists/The-little-homies) It features religious imagery mixed with urban life, such as [Kendrick in priest\'s robes](https://genius.com/11593050) and a moving re-enactment of [Leonardo Da Vinci](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leonardo_da_Vinci)\'s painting [*The Last Supper*](http://www.leonardodavinci.net/the-last-supper.jsp)—juxtaposing this with the concept of humility in the chorus.\\n\\nOn a religious note, the song could also be a reference to [James Chapter 4, verse 7](https://www.biblegateway.com/passage/?search=james+4%3A7&version=NLT):\\n\\n>So humble yourselves before God. It seems to reference the character Deebo\'s theme song from the popular comedy movie [<i>Friday<\/i> (1995)](http://bit.ly/2pA6OFH). Kendrick is also shown riding through the neighborhood on a bicycle in the music video, similar to Deebo in <i>Friday<\/i>.\\n\\nThe song debuted at No. 2 on the Billboard Hot 100 on April 22, 2017, making it not only the highest charting song for Kendrick, but also one of the highest debuting hip-hop singles since [\\\"Love the Way You Lie\\\"](/genius.com/Eminem-love-the-way-you-lie-lyrics) by [Eminem](/artists/Eminem).
